Im walking to the slide with the kid Im watching. When we get there, a kid who cant be much older than four pokes me in the leg.)</em></p> <p><strong>Me:</strong> Oh, hello there!</p> <p><strong>Rude Kid:</strong> Youre too old to be playing on the playground!</p> <p><strong>Me:</strong> Well, Im sorry you feel that way.</p> <p><em>(I was about to turn and guide my kid up the slide, but the rude kid immediately bursts into tears.)</em></p> <p><strong>Me:</strong> Oh, no! Are you okay?</p> <p><strong>Rude Kid:</strong> <em>*runs off bawling*</em></p> <p><em>(I assume thats the last of him, and continue on my way. A few minutes later, however, the rude kid returns with his mom.)</em></p> <p><strong>Mom:</strong> My little sweetums said you made him cry!</p> <p><strong>Me:</strong> <em>*gets a horrible feeling from the use of the word sweetums  has any normal, non-spoiled brat ever been called sweetums?  but stays professional*</em> Im sorry to hear that What did I do?</p> <p><strong>Mom:</strong> He said you kicked tanbark in his face and said his penis was small!</p> <p><strong>Me:</strong> I, <em>uh, </em>what?</p> <p><strong>Rude Kid:</strong> Yeah, I just wanted to touch your booooobs!</p> <p><strong>My Kid:</strong> Your what? <em>*starts giggling*</em> Thats a funny word!</p> <p><strong>Me:</strong> <em>*to My Kid*</em> Ask your mom a little later. Can you go play in the sandbox with [My Kids Friend]? <em>*to Rude Kids mom*</em> Maam, the fact that your son knows these words is a bit odd to me, but I wont question your parenting. Your son told me I was too old for the playground and burst into tears after I acknowledged him.</p> <p><strong>Mom:</strong> <em>*ignoring half of what I said* </em>How do you know what penis and boobs mean?</p> <p><strong>Me:</strong> With all due respect, Im fourteen. Ive had sex ed twice. With that said, Im going to leave this conversation as I see no benefits to continuing it. All I can say is please, please, think about your parenting. Goodbye.</p> <p><em>(We had a relatively good day at the park after that. The lady actually ended up being hauled off after trying to pummel someone who politely asked her sweetums to stop blocking the slide. I really hope I never run into anyone like her ever again.)</em></p> </div> <div id=\"meta_container\"> <div id=\"meta_vote\"><div id=\"post-ratings-44414\" class=\"post-ratings\"
